The hotel beach is quiet during the day, with lots of beach chairs and umbrellas for shade. The two downsides were the breakfast food - there were not many western options and the location, this hotel is situated on the opposite of the island with all the food and pedestrian streets. However, the hotel is right next to a huge outlet mall with numerous options of western clothing shops. We really enjoyed our stay here and would recommend it to any travellers wanting a getaway.

The room is very clean and the facilities are very new. The toiletries are all Jurlique, the hair dryer is also the latest quick-drying type, and the minibar and snacks in the refrigerator are free.
The environment of the hotel's public areas is also very good: the small beach with its own is very photogenic, there are few people, and you can basically enjoy the beach alone. Older children will be very happy to dig sand. Tongmeng Island Children's Park is also very fun. The baby likes the ocean ball very much and is reluctant to leave. Next time, I will arrange a longer time to play.
The Ruoshui Japanese food double set that comes with the package is good, the ingredients are very fresh, and it tastes better than breakfast haha. The breakfast is quite satisfactory, not too amazing.

In general, if you are traveling with young babies or on vacation and are too lazy to run around, this hotel is indeed a good choice. You can basically stay in the hotel to eat, drink and have fun. If you go out, there are many beaches near the hotel. If you are afraid of crowds, it is much more comfortable to choose this place. I will stay here again next time I come to Xiamen and plan to experience the parent-child room.

Here are a few small suggestions to make the guest experience better:
- The free tea bags in the room can be replaced with tea leaves. After all, you are in Fujian, and the room also provides tea sets, but the tea leaves are charged. Tea leaves are not expensive in the first place, and you don‚Äôt have to use precious tea species, but the experience adds points
- Travel photography is provided, but the response speed of the travel photography customer service is really slow. It is not good for taking photos of babies, but it is good for taking photos of girls.
- It has the label of a parent-child hotel. It would be better if breakfast could add some things that babies can eat (such as freshly squeezed juice without additives, waffles and muffins with less sugar, etc.)

The hotel's breakfast is average, with not many varieties, and there are few Western-style breakfasts; the Chinese-style part has Xiamen's local snacks, sand tea noodles, which are worth tasting. Room service is also good. The Japanese restaurant (Ruoshui), the serving is very slow, which is the most dissatisfying part of my trip this time.
Transportation: Due to the relatively remote location of the hotel, you need to take a taxi to go anywhere except the nearby attractions. To do a nucleic acid, you have to take a taxi to a place of 3 or 4 kilometers. This is not very convenient.
